21 pm
 is akashiya ghatana ke didaar ke liye log behad utsuk rahete hai or kai dinon pehle se hi taiyaariyaan shuru kar dete hai

 Indian Army to provide training to women officers of Afghan National Army, training will be given to 20 women officers, 3 week training campaign
 After training the Afghan National Army (ANA) for many years now, Indian Army wants to train women officers of Afghanistan
 
 yuddh se jujh rahe afghanistan kii mahila adhikariyon ko bhartiya sena training dene kii taiyaari main he
 The Indian Army will provide special training to 20 women of the Afghan army at the Officers Training Academy (OTA), Chennai
 mahila adhikariyon ke liye special training modul tay kiya gaya he, jiskaa ve hissaa hongi
 Training will be given in Chennai for the next three weeks
 yah training 25 november se 21 disambar tak di ja rahi he
 This is the third consecutive year that women officers of the Afghan army are being trained at the OTA in Chennai
 army se jude sutron kaa is maamle par kahana he ki yah koi vaarshik training capsule nahin he lekin yah hamarisanya ranneeti kaa hissaa he
 However, due to continuous training for many years, now it has become routine
 sankhya main bhi badhottaree bhi ho sakati he
